<Name>Alizen<//Name><date>1547370564964< /date>< Rate>
5</Rate>
< Text>
Aqua Lounge is an upscale bar located inside the Fashion Island Hotel that offers a great selection of cocktails and some great music.

I came here with a couple of friends after a reception at the hotel and it did not disappoint. The lounge was very busy because of the reception and there was quite a range of people there, but it was definitely more of an older crowd when I went that night.

The bar itself holds about 4 bartenders so you can get your drinks quickly. Their menu has a wonderful selection but my boyfriend and I opted for a jack and coke ($12) and a red bull vodka ($12.40). Both of these were cheaper than their signature cocktails and still had about 2 oz or so per beverage.

Aqua Lounge has a very intimate space with lots of table seating. They have a small dance floor as well with a DJ playing hip hop. I found that the music became a bit repetitive towards the end of the night but I still had an enjoyable time.

Overall, I loved my experience here and prefer Aqua Lounge to Eats in Hotel Irvine. I would definitely consider returning for another event.

Pro tip: make sure to validate your ticket with the valet!</Text>

<user_id>104126960550686269983< /user_id><user_name>Alex Diaz< /user_name><Date>1550357433077< /Date>< Rate>
3<//Rate>
< review>
This is located at the Island Hotel, which is across the street from the Neiman Marcus side of Fashion Island. The place can be spotted by the blueish bar in the middle where all the alcohol is located. There is an inside section as well as a small patio area outside.

My friends and I went during happy hour, which I believe is from 3-6 everyday, and items are 50% off. It was pretty empty when we went, and we decided to sit outside.

I had the Newport Sunset and tried a variety of their appetizers. The Newport Sunset was interesting, but it didn't really stand out for me. We also had the fried spuds, some sort of flatbread, and short rib beignets.

The fried spuds were just french fries with what tasted like truffle oil and parmesan, and it was just okay. I liked the short rib beignets best, there was an interesting flavor and texture that was surprised between the crunchy outside, and the meaty inside of the balls. The horseradish sauce on the outside gave wrapped the whole appetizer up well. The flatbread just tasted like a mediocre pizza for me.<//review>

<text>If you took this place out of Newport Beach it might be ok.  They have a bar, a Dj, seats...and are in a nice hotel.

<Review>During one of the most difficult times for our family, we turned to Chapel of the Chimes for assistance. Funeral services and burial services are separate and you will work with a different advisor for each side. For the funeral, my family worked with a funeral director not familiar with our cultural and religious preferences. Lawrence, our burial services advisor, stepped in to support the items we requested and ensured the funeral director understood the process. The day before the actual funeral, Lawrence reached out with news that the funeral director we worked with was no longer with the organization. We were suddenly in a state of anxiety, worrying that my dad's funeral would be in disarray. Despite the sudden change in plans, Lawrence stepped in as an acting funeral director, taking care of all last-minute items and masterfully coordinating the day-of ceremony. Lawrence even came in on his day off to ensure the inurnment was completed smoothly and timely.

From the start of the process, Lawrence was the epitome of customer service and kindness. His patience, sense of propriety and professionalism were unparalleled. < review>
We have been going to this dentist for about a year, and we really like them. I have a terrible phobia of dentists, to the point where sometimes I just start crying when I sit down in the chair, and Doctor Lee is very gentle and cognizant of your fear. Our first appointment he took the time to figure out what triggers my fear the most (shots, and the sound of the equipment) and was able to mostly avoid the things that freak me out the most. Of course, the cleaning tools are going to make sounds and there's not much he can do about that, but he talked and joked around to try to put me at ease and did the necessary work very very gently. The office staff and dental assistants are all very kind and friendly and professional. I couldn't be happier that we found such a great dentist office that is very convenient to where we live. Also, they are being very thorough and professional with their COVID procedures.< /review>
